<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсобка.html>подсо́бка</a> (22584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подсо́б(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podsób(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсобка.html>подсо́бка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podsóbka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсобка.html>подсо́бки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсобка.html>подсо́бки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсобка.html>подсо́бок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> storeroom, utility room</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-со́вывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sóvyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсовывать.html>подсо́вывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podsóvyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсунуть.html>подсу́нуть</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to palm off <i>(on / upon)</i></li></ol>

***подсознательный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсознательный.html>подсозна́тельный</a> (11108)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сознательный.html>созна́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soznátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсознательный.html>подсозна́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podsoznátelʹnyj</span>)
</p>

***подспудный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подспудный.html>подспу́дный</a> (26546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> спу́дом</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod spúdom</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">under a vessel, bucket (for grains)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matthew_5:15%E2%80%9316" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Matthew 5:15–16">Matthew 5:15</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***подставить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a> (5141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sub-, under</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podstávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подставлять.html>подставля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place under <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to place near <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стул.html>стул</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podstávitʹ</b> stul komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull up a chair for</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold up to, to offer to, to make accessible to <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by bringing or turning something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>другу́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podstávitʹ</b> drugúju ščóku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn the other cheek</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножка.html>но́жку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podstávitʹ</b> nóžku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to trip</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to substitute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expose, to leave vulnerable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> criminology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to frame, to conspire to incriminate falsely a presumably innocent person</li></ol>

***подставлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подставлять.html>подставля́ть</a> (8518)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podstávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">imperfectivizing suffix</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подставлять.html>подставля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podstavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подставить.html>подста́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to place under <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to place near <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подставлять.html>подставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стул.html>стул</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podstavljátʹ</b> stul komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull up a chair for</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold up to, to offer to, to make accessible to <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by bringing or turning something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подставлять.html>подставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>другу́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podstavljátʹ</b> drugúju ščóku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn the other cheek</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подставлять.html>подставля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножка.html>но́жку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podstavljátʹ</b> nóžku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to trip</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to substitute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expose, to leave vulnerable</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подстаканник.html>подстака́нник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podstakánnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подстаканник.html>подстака́нника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подстаканник.html>подстака́нники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подстаканник.html>подстака́нников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tea glass holder
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1993</b>,  Виктор Олегович Пелевин (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Victor_Pelevin" class="extiw" title="w:Victor ***подстегнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подстегнуть.html>подстегну́ть</a> (30441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стегнуть.html>стегну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stegnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подстегнуть.html>подстегну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podstegnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подстёгивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fasten, to clip <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">something to something, usually from below or from the side</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to whip on, to drive forward by whipping</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spur, to motivate to action</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to intensify; to whet (one's appetite)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подстёгивание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podstjógivanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подстёжка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podstjóžka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***подстерегаемый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подстерегаемый.html>подстерега́емый</a> (13699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подстраховать.html>подстрахова́ть</a> (32406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страховать.html>страхова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">straxovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подстраховать.html>подстрахова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podstraxovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подстрахо́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to secure; to insure; to stand by, to spot (in sports)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подстраховать.html>подстраху́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтоб.html>чтоб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Podstraxúj</b> menjá, štob ja ne upál.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Spot me so I don't fall.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подстрекну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podstreknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подстрекать.html>подстрека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podstrekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подстрекну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to incite, to instigate, to set on, to abet</li>
<li>to stir up, to provoke, to excite</li></ol>
